title": "Air fried garlic French fries",
                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Air fried garlic French fries\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#airfriedgarlicfrenchfries #chips #friedgarlic #garlicpotatoes #airfryer #garlicfrenchfries #dry #garlicfies\n|hashtagrev=12032020\n|description=Delicious garlic flavoured chips; A few potatoes, a bulb of garlic and some olive oil\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=1st September 2021\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment =\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  5 minutes\n|CookTime =  35 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 994\n|PortionCalories = 497\n|Image = [[Image:Air fried garlic French fries recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">So Simple, So Garlicky</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This could not be easier - garlic perfection!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n\n[[Garlic]] flavoured [[Chips|chips]]; lovely!  Saw this idea in a Gordon Ramsey Sunday Dinners TV program and as we always make our [[French fries]] in an [[Air Fryer|air fryer]], this was a no-brainer.\n\nA full bulb of [[Garlic|garlic]] sliced in half is plenty - wrap the other half in [[Cling Film|cling film]] for the next time!\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| Half a bulb of [[Garlic|garlic]] - sliced sideways to reveal all the [[Cloves|cloves]]\n| 4 medium sized [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Pinch of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| Pinch of [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Peel the [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| Cut them into [[French fries]] - we use a [[Sopito Stainless Steel Potato Cutter]]\n| Rinse the [[Chips|chips]] well under running water\n| Leave them soaking in [[Salted|salted]] water until you are ready to cook them\n| [[Dry]] the [[Potato chips|potato chips]] in a [[Tea-towel|tea-towel]] or a [[Salad spinner|salad spinner]]\n| Cook them at your [[Air Fryer|air fryer]]'s hottest temperature [200\u00b0 C / 220\u00b0] for 35 minutes or until golden.\n| Shake the [[Cloves|cloves]] out of the 'shell' of the [[Garlic|garlic]] bulb. Discard the shell and keep the golden [[Garlic cloves|garlic cloves]] to serve with the [[Chips|chips]] - Yum!\n}}\n\n\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Air fried garlic French fries chips.jpg|Cooked to perfection - don't waste the lovely garlic cloves!\nImage:Air fried garlic French fries ready to cook.jpg|Ready to cook\nImage:Kuhn Rikon Salad Spinner.jpg|Use a salad spinner to dry the French fries\nImage:Potato chipper.jpg|This comes highly recommended - [[Sopito Stainless Steel Potato Cutter][\n</gallery>\n\n===Chef's notes===\nThis time of year, locally we are limited to [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]] but in season, Cara, [[Markies]], Agria, Mozart and Maris Piper make the best [[Chips|chips]]. &#127839;&#127839;&#127839;\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Air fried recipes]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#airfriedgarlicfrenchfries #chips #friedgarlic #garlicpotatoes #airfryer #garlicfrenchfries #dry #garlicfies</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

The [[Corn|corn]] cobs need to be cut in half to fit in the [[Air fryer|air fryer]], but this is also how they are often sold (in the UK).\n\nThe [[Tefal ActiFry AL806040 Air Fryer]] is still my favourite cooking tool.  It's so ugly it needs to be stored in the conservatory but it's still brought into use a couple of times a week.  It is also a ''must-have'' for the motorhome!\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] cob cut into two halves\n| Pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Butter|butter]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Pop the halved [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] cobs in the airfryer with a teaspoon of [[Butter|butter]] and a pinch of [[Salt|salt]].\n| [[Air fry]] for 20 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a little extra [[Butter|butter]]\n===Chef's notes===\nThe start photograph shown 1 tablespoon of [[Butter|butter]], but that was far too much.  A teaspoonful is all that's needed.  Any more just gets left in the [[Air Fryer|air fryer]] when the food is removed.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Air fried recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#butter #airfryer #airfriedsweetcorncobs #sweetcorn #airfriedrecipes #roast #corn #airfry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Barbecued lime and chili chicken wings",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Barbecued lime and chili chicken wings a Barbecue recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #barbecuedlimeandchilichickenwings #chili #limejuice #marinade #grilled #jaggery #refrigerator #rest #barbecued #drumsticks \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Lime, chili and salt go so well together that I now have a hankering for a Mexican drink!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2070\n|PortionCalories = 345\n|DatePublished=7th February 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Lime and chili chicken wings with Garlic and herb Jerusalem artichokes\n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 40 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Lime and chili chicken wings.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Surprisingly good.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Probably a tad overcooked, but still dammn good.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Lime and chili chicken wings marinading.jpg|300px|thumb|right|Ready to marinate]]\n[[Lime]], [[chili]] and [[salt]] go so well together that I now have a hankering for a Mexican drink!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 kg [2 lb] [[chicken]] thighs or wings, skin on and bone in\n| 125 ml [4 fl oz] freshly squeezed [[lime juice]]\n| 4 fresh red bird's eye [[chillies]], finely chopped\n| &#189; teaspoon [[sea salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[demerara sugar]] or [[jaggery]]\n| 3 teaspoons [[olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the [[lime juice]], [[chili]], [[salt]], [[sugar]] and [[oil]] together in a bowl\n| Cut some deep slashes into the flesh so the [[marinade]] can 'work' on the meat\n| Marinate the [[chicken]] in a [[refrigerator]] for 2 hours or more, turning a few times\n| [[Barbecue]] the chicken for about 15 minutes on a well oiled grill, turning often to prevent burning\n| Check the [[chicken]] is properly cooked before serving\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe with a green salad, [[jacket potatoes]], [[sour cream]] and [[Pickled jalape\u00f1os]]\n===Variations===\nYou could make this with [[chicken thighs]] or [[drumsticks]].  Larger pieces will take a little longer to cook.  Check the juices run clear when the thickest part is pierced with a fork.\n\nThese can also be cooked on an oven tray with a rack at 180\u00b0 C [350\u00b0 F - Gas 4 - Moderate/Medium]. Allow 40 minutes for small pieces like wings. 50 minutes for larger pieces like thighs and drumsticks. Check juices run clear and leave to [[rest]] for 5 minutes before serving.    \nTry this [[marinade]] with [[lamb tenderloin fillets]] or [[king prawns]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:North American recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Marinaded]][[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #barbecuedlimeandchilichickenwings #chili #limejuice #marinade #grilled #jaggery #refrigerator #rest #barbecued #drumsticks </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Barbecue beef short ribs",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Barbecue beef short ribs a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#beefshortribs #barbecuebeefshortribs #marinade #roast #argentineribs #roastingtray #porkspareribs #butter #ribs #oliveoil #chillipowder \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Everyone has tried pork spare ribs, well this is the man-sized version - I have adapted Jamie Oliver's &quot;Daisy Mays barbecue Ribs&quot; from Jamie's great &quot;\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 378\n|PortionCalories = 94\n|DatePublished=18th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 8 hours 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 8 hours\n |Image = [[Image:Barbecue beef short ribs recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Naughty, but nice</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Thesee are great, but still quite an expensive meal in my opine.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nEveryone has tried [[Pork spare ribs|pork spare ribs]], well this is the man-sized version - I have adapted Jamie Oliver's \"Daisy Mays barbecue [[Ribs]]\" from Jamie's great \"America book\" (ISBN 0718154762).  We had similar ribs to this at Bodean's [[Barbecue]] Restaurant, by The Tower of London, after a [http://www.walks.com/London_Walks_Home/Saturdays_Walks/default.aspx#12939 Jack The Ripper walk] with some great friends of ours.\n\nThis recipe takes 8 hours to cook, so make sure that you allow enough time!\n\nAsk your butcher for '[[beef short ribs]] from the plate', or [[Argentine ribs]]. You don't want back ribs as these are not the same.  I understand from talking to a butcher that this particular cut of [[beef]] is also known as 'Jacob's ladder'.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| A halved 4 bone rack of [[beef short ribs]] 'from the plate', (about 1kg)\n| 5 tablespoons [[American squeezy mustard]]\n}}\n'''there's the rub'''\n* 2 teaspoons [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]] (or to taste)\n* 4 tablespoons [[Spanish]] [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]]\n* &#189; tablespoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n* &#189; tablespoon [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]]\n* 2 tablespoons [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e\n* 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n* 2 tablespoons ruby [[port]]\n'''here's the [[Marinade|marinade]]'''\n* 4 tablespoons [[muscovado sugar]]\n* 2 tablespoons good [[Honey|honey]], warmed in the [[Microwave|microwave]] for a few seconds to make it runny\n* 1 tablespoon [[Butter|butter]]\n* 1 beef [[Oxo cube]], crumbled\n* 2 tablespoons water\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 120\u00b0 C (250\u00b0 F - gas &frac12;)\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Beef_short_ribs_rub_8_hours.jpg|After 8 hours\nImage:Beef_short_ribs_rub_7_hours.jpg|After 7 hours\nImage:Beef_short_ribs_rub_covered.jpg|Meat-side up, covered in the rub\nImage:Beef_short_ribs.jpg|1.1kg of [[beef short ribs]], bone-side up\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Make shallow criss-cross cuts on the meats side of the ribs.\n| Mix the rub ingredients together in a bowl and mix well.\n| Paint this all over the meat, getting it into all of the cuts and areas where your butcher has removed excess fat.\n| If you have the time, place the ribs in a [[Lock and Lock]] style box and leave in a cool lace for a few hours before you start the cooking process.\n| Pop the ribs in a lightly greased [[roasting tray]], bone-side down, cover the tin with a layer of [[baking foil]] and [[Roast|roast]] for 6 hours.\n| After 6 hours, remove the tin-foil covering, drain and reserve and refrigerate the juices, they make a wonderful chilli-beef dripping!\n| Gently heat the [[Marinade|marinade]] ingredients in a small pan, stirring until you have a liquid mix.\n| Tear a few large sheets of really strong [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]] ([[Tin-foil#Heavy-duty tin foil|Bacofoil Classic]] is ideal as it's so thick and strong).\n| Put the ribs in the foil, bone-side up and paint the [[Marinade|marinade]] all over with a silicone [[Brush|brush]].  \n| Fold the foil over so you have a sealed parcel.\n| Wrap in the second sheet of [[Foil|foil]] and put back in the [[roasting tray]] for a further hour.\n| After the hour in the foil parcel, increase the heat to 140\u00b0 C (257\u00b0 F - gas 1), fold back the foil roast the ribs, uncovered and [[Roast|roast]] for another 40 minutes, basting often with the syrupy marinade.\n| Remove and rest for at least 15 minutes before serving.\n}}\n\n===Chef's notes===\nI've found it difficult to obtain [[beef short ribs]] from anywhere but a specialist butchers and even then, they needed to be ordered in advance.  Today, I was delighted to discover [[F. Conisbee specialist butchers]] had them in stock. 4 [[Argentine ribs]] for \u00a321.04.  Robert cut them in half again lengthwise with the bandsaw. One of these half-ribs per person is plenty!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beefshortribs #barbecuebeefshortribs #marinade #roast #argentineribs #roastingtray #porkspareribs #butter #ribs #oliveoil #chillipowder </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Black bean burritos recipe Cooking with chillies\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#beans #sourcream #blackbeanburritos #salsa #burritos #bean #chillies #baking #emmenthalcheese #sweetcorn #cheese \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a quick-to-make recipe that uses prepared ingredients, but still allows you to tailor it to your particular taste\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1823\n|PortionCalories = 303\n|DatePublished=8th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6 - Makes 6 [[Burrito|burritos]]\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Black bean burritos recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Better than El Paso!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Much nicer than the prepared versions</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThis is a quick-to-make recipe that uses prepared ingredients, but still allows you to tailor it to your particular taste.  [[Emmenthal cheese]] is obviously not authentic, but I just love it, so [[Emmenthal]] it is.  Use any [[Cheese|cheese]] of your choice.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 pack of [[Flour|flour]] [[Tortillas|tortillas]]\n| 175 g can of [[Black beans|black beans]]\n| 165 g can of [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] kernels\n| 350 g bottle of [[Tomato salsa|tomato salsa]]\n| 150 ml tub of [[Sour cream|sour cream]]\n| 200g [[Emmenthal cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 3 fresh or [[Pickled|pickled]] [[Red chillies|red chillies]] (or to taste)\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| [[Olive oil]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Tip the [[Salsa|salsa]] into a bowl\n| Chop the [[Chillies|chillies]] finely, remove the [[Seeds|seeds]] if you don't want it too hot.\n| Rinse and drain the [[Black beans|black beans]]\n| Place 2/3rds of the [[Beans|beans]] in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade and blend to a chunky paste\n| Add the blended [[Beans|beans]] and the remaining whole [[Beans|beans]] to the bowl\n| Add the [[Salsa|salsa]] to the bowl, stir in the [[Chillies|chillies]] and mix well\n| Reserve about 4 tablespoons of the [[Bean|bean]]/[[Salsa|salsa]] mix to a saucer to top the [[Burritos|burritos]]\n| Rinse and drain the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] and add to the bowl of [[Beans|beans]] with 2/3rds of the [[Sour cream|sour cream]] and mix well.  Keep the rest of the [[Cream|cream]] to serve with the [[Burritos|burritos]]\n| Lightly [[Oil|oil]] a [[Baking|baking]] dish\n| Fill 6 [[Tortillas|tortillas]] with the [[Bean|bean]] mix from the bowl, roll them up and place in the [[Baking|baking]] dish, seam-side down\n| Spread the reserved [[Bean|bean]] mixture from the saucer over the [[Burritos|burritos]] and cover with [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| [[Bake]] for 20 minutes or until heated through.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with the remaining [[Sour cream|sour cream]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Cuban recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beans #sourcream #blackbeanburritos #salsa #burritos #bean #chillies #baking #emmenthalcheese #sweetcorn #cheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Boston baked beans",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Boston baked beans, Barbecue recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#bostonbakedbeans #beans #porkbelly #bake #muscovadosugar #muslin #chillibeans #mustardpowder #darksoysauce #molasses #haricotbeans \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The results from this classic recipe for Boston baked beans are fantastic, nothing like canned baked beans\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2749\n|PortionCalories = 458\n|DatePublished=27th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Boston baked beans, fillet steak & kettle crisps\n |Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 18 hours\n |PrepTime = 12 hours 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 5 hours 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Boston baked beans and steak.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Beans from Boston</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">These are the best Boston beans!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThe results from this classic recipe for Boston baked beans are fantastic, nothing like canned baked beans.  As the [[Beans|beans]] need an overnight soaking, you need to start this recipe a day in advance.  This is a very hearty recipe and you'll find that a little goes a long way.\n\nThese also [[freeze]] really well.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500g (1lb 2oz) [[Dried|dried]] white [[Haricot beans|haricot beans]]\n| 400g (14oz) strip of [[Pork belly|pork belly]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Muscovado sugar]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Molasses|molasses]] or [[Black treacle|black treacle]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Mustard powder|mustard powder]]\n| 2 [[clove buds]]\n| 3 or 4 large shallots peeled or 2 small onions, peeled and quartered\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 3 tablespoons of [[tomato pur\u00e9e]] \n| 2 teaspoons of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] or to taste\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Soak the [[Beans|beans]] overnight in cold water, refreshing the water a few times if you are able.\n* 20 minutes before you're ready to cook, preheat the [[oven]] to 140\u00b0 C (257\u00b0 F - gas 1), [fan oven 120\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Boston baked beans, baked.jpg|Stir and serve!\nImage:Boston beans ready to bake.jpg|Ready to bake\nImage:Boston baked beans ingredients.jpg|The basic ingredients\n</gallery>\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Drain and rinse the soaked [[Beans|beans]] a few times in fresh cold water.\n| Place in a large pan and cover by about 5 cm (2\") of cold water - don't add any [[Salt|salt]] .\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and boil vigorously for 15 minutes, reduce the heat, cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 1 hour\n| This stage takes only 15 minutes if cooked in a [[pressure cooker]], see: [[How to cook beans or pulses in a pressure cooker]]\n| Drain the [[Beans|beans]] reserving the liquor\n| Add the [[Beans|beans]] to a large [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]]\n| Remove the rind from the [[Pork belly|pork belly]] in one piece and add to the beans.  Leaving it whole makes it easier to remove and discard at the end of the cooking process.\n| Cut the pork belly into into 2.5cm (1\") chunks and stir into the [[Beans|beans]]\n| Push the cloves into one of the onion pieces or into a [[muslin]] bag so they can be easily retrieved\n| [[Salt]] aside, mix the remaining ingredients into a few cups of the liquor and add to the [[Beans|beans]]\n| If required, top up with hot water so the beans are barely covered\n| Cover with the lid and [[Bake|bake]] for 3 hours\n| After 3 hours remove the lid add a little more liquor if needed, bring the [[Pork|pork]] chunks to the surface, increase the oven temperature to 180\u00b0C (350\u00b0F, Gas 4) and [[Bake|bake]] uncovered for 1 to 1.5 hours, checking every 15 minutes until it reaches your desired consistency.\n| remove the large onion pieces and the [[cloves]] and discard the pork rind.\n| Season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] or [[soy sauce]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with crusty [[Bread|bread]] or as an [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] to [[Barbecued|barbecued]] [[Meats|meats]].\n===Chef's notes===\nThese will keep for a few weeks if [[Refrigerated|refrigerated]] in a [[Lock & Lock box]].\n===Variations===\nProbably not authentic but I added a little [[dark soy sauce]] and some [[chili sauce]] when adjusting the final seasoning.\n==See also==\n* [[Chilli beans]]\n* http://www.deliaonline.com/recipes/cuisine/exotic/american/boston-baked-beans.html\n* http://www.bbc.co.uk/food/recipes/bostonbakedbeans_10471\n* http://www.channel4.com/4food/recipes/tv-show-recipes/the-fabulous-baker-brothers-recipes/baker-brother-beans-recipe\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#bostonbakedbeans #beans #porkbelly #bake #muscovadosugar #muslin #chillibeans #mustardpowder #darksoysauce #molasses #haricotbeans </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

The [[Batter|batter]] can be made in about 15 minutes, so they are suitable as a last-minute addition to a [[Breakfast|breakfast]]. They are made fluffy by beating the [[Egg whites|egg whites]] separately and folding them in as the last step.\n\nYou may find it easier to weight the liquids as 354ml of [[Milk|milk]] is roughly 354g, etc.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 3 [[free range eggs]], separated\n| 354 ml (1.5) cups [[Milk|milk]]\n| 225g (1/2 lb) ''approx. 1 &#190; cups' [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Baking powder|baking powder]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| 60 ml (1/4 cup) [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Heat the waffle maker / waffle machine / waffle [[Iron|iron]]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Mix [[Egg yolks|egg yolks]] and [[Milk|milk]].\n| Add [[Flour|flour]], [[Baking powder|baking powder]], [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Salt|salt]] and mix well.\n| Add the [[Oil|oil]].\n| Beat the [[Egg whites|egg whites]] until stiff and then fold into the [[Batter|batter]].\n| Lightly [[Spray|spray]] the non-stick plates with [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]].\n| Pour about 1 cup of [[Batter|batter]] into the waffle maker and close the lid.\n| Close and cook until the lights indicate the waffle is cooked or until the waffle stops steaming - about 5 minutes.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* http://en.wikibooks.org/wiki/Cookbook:Breakfast_Waffles\n==See also==\n\n* {{SeeAlso-Waffles}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belgian recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#breakfastwaffles #batter #vegetableoil #eggwhites #bakingpowder #breakfast #eggyolks #flour #griddled #miseenplace #freerangeeggs </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Caesar salad",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Caesar salad, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#salad #oliveoil #worcestershiresauce #caesarsalad #anchovies #lettuce #egg #garlic #blackpepper #parmesancheese #croutons \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A typical Caesar salad comprises romaine lettuce and croutons dressed with parmesan cheese, lemon juice, olive oil, egg, Worcestershire sauce, and\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 763\n|PortionCalories = 190\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 as a snack, or 6 as a [[Starter|starter]] / side [[Salad|salad]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 5 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Caesar salad recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wheel out that Hostess Trolley.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.9</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This recipe deserves to be served properly! \ud83d\ude01</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nA typical Caesar [[Salad|salad]] comprises romaine [[Lettuce|lettuce]] and [[croutons]] dressed with [[Parmesan cheese|parmesan cheese]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Egg|egg]], [[Worcestershire sauce]], and [[Black pepper|black pepper]] originally prepared tableside. Caesar Cardini (Italian-born [[Mexican]]) is credited with creating the salad.\n\nContrary to popular belief, the original Caesar's [[Salad|salad]] recipe did not contain pieces of [[Anchovy|anchovy]]; the slight anchovy flavour comes from the [[Worcestershire sauce]]. Cardini was opposed to using [[Anchovies|anchovies]] in his salad.\n\nIn the book From Julia Child's Kitchen, Julia Child describes how she ate a Caesar's [[Salad|salad]] at Cardini's restaurant when she was a child in 1920s, and some 50 years later she sought out and called Cardini's daughter, in order to discover the original recipe. In this recipe, [[Lettuce|lettuce]] leaves are served whole on the plate, because they are meant to be lifted by the stem and eaten with the fingers. It also calls for coddled [[Eggs|eggs]] and Italian [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n\nRather than re create the absolute original recipe, I have chosen to go for a composite of many current 'favourite' recipes.\n\n\n'''[[Salad]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 small cos [[Lettuce|lettuce]], washed and separated into leaves\n| 1 50 g (2 oz) can of [[Anchovy fillets|anchovy fillets]], drained. Keep 3 back for the dressing as well as the reserved [[Oil|oil]]\n| 40 g (1.5 oz) [[Parmesan cheese]], freshly and finely [[Grated|grated]]\n}}\n'''Dressing'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]]\n| 1 clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled\n| [[Juice]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]] or [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[English mustard powder]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Worcestershire sauce]]\n| 150 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n'''Cro\u00fbtons'''\n| 2 slices of thick white [[Bread|bread]], crusts removed and cut into bite-sized cubes\n| 1 [[Clove garlic, crushed|clove garlic, crushed]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n'''Cro\u00fbtons'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[croutons]] to a [[Frying pan|frying pan]], season with [[Black pepper|black pepper]], start the [[Garlic|garlic]] sizzling then add the cro\u00fbtons. Toss and [[Fry|fry]] until crispy and to taste\n}}\n'''Dressing'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Egg|egg]], [[Garlic|garlic]] clove, [[Lime juice|lime juice]], [[Mustard powder|mustard powder]], [[Worcestershire sauce]] and the 3 reserved [[Anchovies|anchovies]] and blend until smooth. Gradually drizzle the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] into the [[Blender|blender]] as though you were making mayonaise. As long as you don't rush adding the [[Oil|oil]], you should have a  [[Sauce|sauce]], the consistency of runny [[Salad|salad]]-[[Cream|cream]].\n}}\n'''Final assembly'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Finely chop the [[Anchovies|anchovies]]\n| Leaving the leaves whole, but ripping up very big leaves, layer the [[Salad|salad]] leaves and [[Anchovies|anchovies]]\n| Drizzle with the dressing and sprinkle with [[Parmesan]], finishing with the cro\u00fbtons.\n}}\n===Variations===\n*Add a handful of [[Wild rocket leaves|wild rocket leaves]] for a spicier [[Salad|salad]].\n*Add sliced cooked chicken or turkey for a more substantial meal.\n*Leave out the anchovies for a vegetarian version and use a vegetarian [[Worcestershire sauce]] - the original contains anchovies.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#salad #oliveoil #worcestershiresauce #caesarsalad #anchovies #lettuce #egg #garlic #blackpepper #parmesancheese #croutons </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

Caesar Cardini (Italian-born [[Mexican]]) is credited with creating the salad.\n\nContrary to popular belief, the original Caesar's [[Salad|salad]] recipe did not contain pieces of [[Anchovy|anchovy]]; the slight anchovy flavour comes from the [[Worcestershire sauce]]. Cardini was opposed to using [[Anchovies|anchovies]] in his salad.\n\nIn the book From Julia Child's Kitchen, Julia Child describes how she ate a Caesar's [[Salad|salad]] at Cardini's restaurant when she was a child in 1920s, and some 50 years later she sought out and called Cardini's daughter, in order to discover the original recipe. In this recipe, [[Lettuce|lettuce]] leaves are served whole on the plate, because they are meant to be lifted by the stem and eaten with the fingers. It also calls for coddled [[Eggs|eggs]] and Italian [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n\nRather than re create the absolute original recipe, I have chosen to go for a composite of many current 'favourite' recipes.\n\n\n'''[[Salad]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 small cos [[Lettuce|lettuce]], washed and separated into leaves\n| 40 g (1.5 oz) [[Parmesan cheese]], freshly and finely [[Grated|grated]]\n}}\n'''Dressing'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]]\n| 1 clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled\n| [[Juice]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]] or [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[English mustard powder]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Worcestershire sauce]]\n| 150 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''Cro\u00fbtons'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 slices of thick white [[Bread|bread]], crusts removed and cut into bite-sized cubes\n| 1 [[Clove garlic, crushed|clove garlic, crushed]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n'''Cro\u00fbtons'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[croutons]] to a [[Frying pan|frying pan]], season with [[Black pepper|black pepper]], start the [[Garlic|garlic]] sizzling then add the cro\u00fbtons. Toss and [[Fry|fry]] until crispy and to taste\n}}\n'''Dressing'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Egg|egg]], [[Garlic|garlic]] clove, [[Lime juice|lime juice]], [[Mustard powder|mustard powder]], [[Worcestershire sauce]] and the 3 reserved [[Anchovies|anchovies]] and bland until smooth. Gradually drizzle the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] into the [[Blender|blender]] as though you were making [[mayonnaise]]. As long as you don't rush adding the [[Oil|oil]], you should have a  [[Sauce|sauce]], the consistency of runny [[Salad cream]].\n}}\n'''Final assembly'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Leaving the leaves whole, but ripping up very big leaves, layer the [[Salad|salad]] leaves and [[Anchovies|anchovies]]\n| Drizzle with the dressing and sprinkle with [[Parmesan]], finishing with the cro\u00fbtons.\n}}\n===Variations===\n*Add a handful of [[Wild rocket leaves|wild rocket leaves]] for a spicier [[Salad|salad]].\n*Add sliced cooked chicken or turkey for a more substantial meal.\n*For a vegetarian version use a vegetarian [[Worcestershire sauce]] - the original contains anchovies.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#salad #oliveoil #worcestershiresauce #anchovies #lettuce #garlic #egg #croutons #parmesancheese #blackpepper #wildrocketleaves </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
}

                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Caesar sauce - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#thermomix #sauce #garlic #lemonjuice #mustard #mayonnaise #oliveoil #egg #parmesancheese #worcestershiresauce #grated \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This Caesar sauce recipe is a translation of a recipe in Salsas y Alinos con Thermomix (Susaeta Ediciones)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1133\n|PortionCalories = 188\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = The new [[Thermomix]] TM5 (2014)\n |Servings = Servings: 6 - Makes 400 ml\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 5 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = none\n |Image = [[Image:The new (2014) Thermomix TM5.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Eggy, creamy salad</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Yumm!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a translation of a Caesar sauce recipe in '''Salsas y Ali\u00f1os con [[Thermomix]] (Susaeta Ediciones)'''\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| 4 [[Anchovy fillets|anchovy fillets]]\n| 2 [[Egg yolks|egg yolks]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Mustard|mustard]]\n| 300g [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 50g [[Sherry vinegar]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Worcestershire sauce]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the peeled [[Garlic|garlic]] in the TM and chop for a '''few seconds / Speed 6'''.\n| Next, add the remaining ingredients, except the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Blend|blend]] '''20 seconds /Speed 5'''.\n| Scrape down the inside of the TM bowl with the spatula.\n| Run the machine at '''Speed 4''' and add the [[Oil|oil]], little by little to the lid so that the [[Sauce|sauce]] is emulsified as if it were a [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nIt goes well with all kinds of [[Salad|salad]], especially the one which carries its name, made with various [[Lettuce|lettuce]] leaves, [[Croutons|croutons]] and [[Boiled|boiled]] [[Egg|egg]].\n===Variations===\nIt is believed that [[Caesar salad|caesar salad]] came into being in July 1920 in the Cesar Palace Hotel, in Tijuana ([[Mexico]]) by the Cardini brothers, the hotel\u0092s chefs and proprietors.  Also, it is known to have been made without the [[Anchovies|anchovies]].  These were added much later to give the [[Sauce|sauce]] more body. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#thermomix #sauce #garlic #lemonjuice #mustard #mayonnaise #oliveoil #egg #parmesancheese #worcestershiresauce #grated </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Cajun Chicken Noodle Stir Fry That sounds weird!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=18th December 2019\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  3 hours, 17 minutes\n|PrepTime =  3 hours, 5 minutes\n|CookTime =  12 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 467\n|PortionCalories = 23\n|Image = [[Image:Cajun Chicken Stir Fry recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">This was good - I remember making it</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And I can taste it from the photograph!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning chicken pieces, air-fried.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After 10 minutes in the air fryer basket]]\n[[Image:Cajun Seasoning, Lime Juice, Olive oil mixed.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After shaking the sealed box for 10 seconds]]\n[[Image:Cajun Seasoning, Lime Juice, Olive oil.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning, olive oil and lime juice]]\nAnother experiment with [[Taste Sensation Seasonings]].\nCajun Chicken Noodle Stir Fry! That sounds weird, but I bet it will be fine.  I marinaded the chicken slices in lime juice for an hour, then added the Cajun Seasoning and a tablespoon of olive oil to a Lock and Lock box, closed the lid and shook for ten seconds.  This leaves the chicken perfectly coated.  It could be stir fried on a wok but I'm going to air fry it in the basket so it can be cooked with no extra oil.\n\nI've used the remains of the Morrisons pre-packed [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] ingredients from yesterday's [[Chilli and lime chicken stir fry]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 large [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]], cut into thin strips\n| 2 tablespoons of [[lime juice]]\n| 1 heaped tablespoon of [[Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning]]\n| 3 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Half a packet of [[Bean sprouts|bean sprouts]] [180 g]\n| Half a packet of fresh [[Egg noodles|egg noodles]] [205 g]\n| Half a packet of Sweet & Crunchy [[Stir fry|stir fry]] [300 g]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* If you get the chance, marinade the chicken pieces in lime juice for an hour before you add the Cajun Seasoning\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Pop the sliced [[Chicken|chicken]] in a [[Lock and Lock box|lock and lock box]] together with the [[Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning]] and one of the tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]].  Shake like crazy to mix.  Leave to [[Marinade|marinade]] for a while longer if you can.\n| This is quicker and easier if you have two woks, if not cook the [[Chicken|chicken]] first and keep warm while you cook the [[Vegetables|vegetables]]\n| [[Stir fry]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] in a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], turning regularly until the chicken is properly cooked - about 5 minutes or longer if it's thickly sliced\n| [[Stir-fry]] the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] in a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] until they are wilted\n| Toss in the [[Beans|beans]] shoots and [[Noodles|noodles]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] until cooked - about 4 minutes\n| Mix in the cooked [[Chicken|chicken]] and serve immediately\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can also cook the [[Chicken|chicken]] in an air-fryer basket for about 5 minutes, instead of pan-[[Frying|frying]]\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#chicken #oliveoil #tastesensationcajunseasoning #vegetables #stirfry #chickenbreast #poultryrecipes #noodles #vegetablerecipes #chineserecipes #northamericanrecipes</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Can-can chicken",
                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Can-can chicken, a fruit recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cancanchicken #butter #chicken #lime #blackpeppercorns #szechuanpeppercorns #mortarandpestle #beer #tablesalt #herb #herbs \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I've long believed that the success of beer can chicken was down to the cooking method rather than the beer itself\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3595\n|PortionCalories = 599\n|DatePublished=7th November 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  2 hours\n|PrepTime =  30 minutes\n|CookTime =  1 hour, 30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Can-can chicken recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Try this, try this, try this..</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This is so simple and so good.  You don't even need beer in the tin. Water will do, drink the beer!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nI've long believed that the success of [[Beer can chicken|beer can chicken]] was down to the cooking method rather than the [[Beer|beer]] itself.  This recipe proves this, conclusively.  It's also ideal if you don't happen to be a [[Beer|beer]] drinker.  All you need is a clean empty tin-can label removed and well washed - the dishwasher is ideal. Use a ring-pull type can as there are less sharp edges to worry about.  I used a cat-food tin!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 2 kg whole [[Chicken|chicken]] (4 lb)\n| 1 [[Lemon]], quartered\n| 1 [[Lime]], half quartered, the remainder sliced for a garnish\n| 1 small bulb of [[Garlic crushed|garlic crushed]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Butter|butter]] at room temperature\n| A huge handful of [[Herbs|herbs]] of your choice\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Black peppercorns|black peppercorns]], roughly crushed in a [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]]\n| [[Table salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Szechuan peppercorns|Szechuan peppercorns]], roughly crushed in a [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Tin-can chicken ready to roast.jpg|Tin-foil hat, ready to roast\nImage:Lemon, lime, herbs and a butter-rub.jpg|The clean empty can, citrus, herbs, water and a the herb-butter rub\nImage:Can-can chicken_ingredients.jpg|Can-can chicken, the ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| This is best made with a [[Grillpro Stainless Steel Chicken Roaster]] - it can be done without (see here).  Just be careful that it does not fall over\n| Add the crushed [[Peppercorns|peppercorns]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] to the warmed [[Butter|butter]], mix well and season with &#188; teaspoons of [[Salt|salt]]\n| Pack the clean empty tin can with the [[Herbs|herbs]], all of the quartered [[Lemons|lemons]] and half the [[Lime|lime]]\n| Half fill with cold water\n| Remove the [[Parsons nose|parsons nose]], if you remember!\n| Carefully sit the [[Chicken|chicken]] on the tin can\n| From the top of the [[Chicken|chicken]], push your fingers between the skin and the breasts to separate them and create pockets.  Pack most of the [[Herb|herb]] [[Butter|butter]] between the skin and the breast mat.  This gives it wonderful flavour and keeps it moist.\n| Rub the remaining [[Herb|herb]] [[Butter|butter]] over the skin and season with a little [[Table salt|table salt]].\n| Make a [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]] 'hat' to protect the bird from burning as it's likely to be quite close to the top of the [[Oven|oven]].\n| [[Roast]] for 1 hour 30 minutes, removing the [[Foil|foil]] for the final 30 minutes.\n| Leave to [[Rest for|rest for]] 15 minutes before serving - I usually turn the [[Oven|oven]] off and leave the door open.\n| Discard the can and its contents, carve and serve.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the [https://www.cookipedia.co.uk/calories/chicken/bq/11#jump chicken] with [[Roast potatoes|roast potatoes]], [[Green vegetables|green vegetables]], gravy and slices of [[Lime|lime]].\n===Chef' notes===\nThis was fantastic - Crisp, juicy and loads of flavour.  It also saves you wasting a can of beer!\n===Variations===\nUse  whatever [[Fresh herbs|fresh herbs]] you can lay your hands on.  I used [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], a huge bunch of [[Sage|sage]], [[Chives|chives]], [[Cutting celery|cutting celery]] and a little [[Thyme|thyme]] - it's surprising how much you can pack into a tin with the [[Lemons|lemons]].\n\nIf you don't have [[Szechuan peppercorns]] use a little more [[black peppercorns]] - I just find they make an interesting change.\n{{Template:Beercan chicken - See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cancanchicken #butter #chicken #lime #blackpeppercorns #szechuanpeppercorns #mortarandpestle #beer #tablesalt #herb #herbs </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

set aside.\n| Using an electric [[Mixer|mixer]], [[Cream|cream]] [[Butter|butter]] and [[Sugar|sugar]].\n| While [[Mixer|mixer]] is running, add [[Eggs|eggs]], one at a time, beating well after each addition.\n| Add [[Corn|corn]], [[Pineapple|pineapple]] and [[Cheese|cheese]];                         "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Cheese and chilli cornbread a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cheeseandchillicornbread #sweetcorn #onions #cheese #bakingpowder #bake #greaseproofpaper #eggs #cornbread #butter #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This savoury cornbread could be served as an accompaniment to a main course or barbecue, as a starter or just as a really nice savoury nibble\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3404\n|PortionCalories = 340\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 10\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Cheese and chilli cornbread recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tasty, but heavy going</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.1</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice, but too much gives me indigestion - and I always eat too much!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis savoury [[Cornbread|cornbread]] could be served as an [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] to a [[Main course|main course]] or  [[Barbecue|barbecue]], as a [[Starter|starter]] or just as a really nice savoury nibble.  It is based on Jamie Oliver's recipe of the same name, though I recall having to adjust the quantities quite a bit from his original recipe.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 60 g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 2 large [[Onions|onions]], peeled and thinly sliced\n| 1 350g can of [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] kernels, drained\n| 4 large [[Eggs|eggs]], beaten\n| 325 g coarse [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]]\n| 250 ml full [[Fat|fat]] [[Milk|milk]]\n| 1 heaped teaspoon [[Baking powder|baking powder]]\n| 6 tablespoons [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| [[Sea Salt|Sea salt]] & [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 150 g strong [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| 3 fresh [[Green chillies|green chillies]], 2 deseeded and chopped finely, the other cut into thin rings\n| [[Olive oil]] for greasing\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Butter|butter]] to a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or [[Wok|wok]], give it a good grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] for 15 minutes\n| Once the [[Onions|onions]] are golden, carefully add the drained [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]]\n| [[Stir-fry]] the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] for a few minutes then remove the pan from the heat and set to one side.\n| Add the [[Eggs|eggs]], [[milk]], [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]], [[Flour|flour]], [[Baking powder|baking powder]], a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and most of the [[Cheese|cheese]] (leaving a little to sprinkle on the top) and beat until really well mixed.\n| Stir in the onions and sweetcorn and mix again.  It helps to leave the mixure to rest for 10 minutes after the first mix to allow the cornmeal to soak up the milk.\n| Grease two 22cm round flan sandwich tins with a little [[Olive oil|olive oil]], line the base with [[Greaseproof paper|greaseproof paper]] and pour in the [[Cornbread|cornbread]] mixture.\n| [[Bake]] for 20 minutes then carefully remove from the oven and sprinkle the top with the remaining sliced [[Chilies|chilies]] and [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| [[Bake]] for a further 10 minutes.\n| Remove from the [[baking tray]] and allow to cool on a wire rack for 15 minutes before serving.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Cheese and chilli cornbread ready to bake.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Cheese and chilli cornbread, ready to bake\nImage:Cheese and chilli cornbread ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The ingredients for cheese and chilli cornbread\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot or cold\n===Chef's note===\nDon't forget the [[greaseproof paper]] or you will find it very hard to get the cornbread out of the tins. :-(\n==See also==\nThis recipe is based on a version of Jamie Olivers 'Chilli cheese cornbread' from ''Jamie's America'' ISBN 978-0718154769\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cheeseandchillicornbread #sweetcorn #onions #cheese #bakingpowder #bake #greaseproofpaper #eggs #cornbread #butter #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

            }

 [[Cheese pupusas|pupusas]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 [[flour]] [[tortillas]]\n| 115g (4 oz)  thinly sliced cooked [[ham]]\n| 115g (4 oz)  [[grated]] [[Emmental]] or [[Gruyere cheese]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[double cream]]\n| 1 tablespoon chopped [[gherkins]] or [[capers]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the [[grated]] [[cheese]] and [[double cream]]\n| Roughly chop the [[ham]] and stir into the [[cheese]] mixture\n| Heat 1 [[tortilla]] in a large heavy based [[frying]] pan\n| Place a quarter of the mixture in the centre of the tortilla\n| Cook for a minute or two\n| Fold [[tortilla]] in half, flip it over and cook for another minute\n| Keep warm while you cook the remaining quesadillas\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[salad]] or [[curtido]]\n===Variations===\nAdd some chopped pickled [[Jalape\u00f1o chillies]] if you like it spicy\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Starters|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:North American recipes|Quesadillas]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortilla #cheese #cheeseandhamquesadillas #doublecream #ham #grated #cornflour #flour #capers #panfried #gherkins </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chicago deep pan pizza",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicago deep pan pizza pie recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#parmesancheese #pizzadough #dried #mushrooms #chicagodeeppanpizza #chorizo #dough #tomatoes #cheddarcheese #grated #mozzarella \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The inspiration for this deep pan pizza pie recipe came from Julia's I believe I Can Fry recipe blog\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1909\n|PortionCalories = 477\n|DatePublished=23rd December 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = ''Sorry Julia, for stealing the fork idea!''\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 25 minutes\n|PrepTime =  40 minutes\n|CookTime =  45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chicago deep pan pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\nThe inspiration for this recipe came from [[I believe I can fry|Julia's I believe I Can Fry recipe blog]]. For me though, the essential deep pan Chicago pizza comes not from Tortuga's but from Bob M. Payton's 300 seat 'Chicago Pizza Pie Factory', deep-down in the basement, in a corner of London's Hanover Square.  It would have been in 1980-something, when mobile phones were the size of car batteries and the Internet was unknown.\n\nIn those days the queues would reach all the way down the stairs to a 'boxing-ring', where you would stand and take your pre-meal drinks.  The Chicago Pizza Pie Factory was a forerunner of Hard-Rock style themed restaurants. Loud rock music played and big screens showed American sports. The decor of the place was authentic Chicago Americana and the food was fantastic with super-slick service that used a really clever idea - A flashing neon sign: 'My Kinda Town'. The flickering letter would indicate to the waitresses which table area of the huge restaurant had food ready to be served.\n\nBob died in the mid 90's and I believe the restaurant closed around that time too.  I notice that a restaurant of the same name exists in Dublin.  I would be interested to see if it bears any resemblance to the original.\n\nThis was absolutely fantastic and nothing like as difficult as you might think.  Thanks for the inspiration Julia - I believe you can!\n===How to ensure a crispy base===\nHaving made these deep pan pizzas many, many times, I've found that sometimes it's hard to get the base well cooked without burning the rest of the [[pizza dough]].  I've found the best way is to use a metal-based pan, similar to a baking tray.  The metal base gets hot enough to crisp the base properly.  I have a cast iron  rectangular Le Creuset baking tray that is absolutely ideal.  It seems a shame as it will mean I'll never use my earthenware deep pan pizza dish again!\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Cooking the chorizo sausage.jpg\nImage:Chicago chorizo pie pizza cheese.jpg\nImage:Chicago chorizo pie pizza filled.jpg\nImage:Chicago chorizo pie pizza topping.jpg\nImage:Chicago pizza pie ready to bake.jpg\nImage:Chicago pizza pie baked.jpg\n</gallery>\n[[Image:ChickenDeepPanPizza.jpg|300px|thumb|right|A chicken and sweetcorn deep pan pizza version, cooked in a Le Creuset pan]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| The sausage-meat removed from 400g of uncooked [[Chorizo]] style [[sausages]] - ''these are not cured so need to be pre cooked''\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], chopped finely\n| 1 portion of [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]]\n| [[Fine yellow cornmeal]] for dusting\n| 110 g (4 oz) [[Cheddar cheese]], [[Grated|grated]]\n| A big handful of fresh [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], brushed and sliced\n| 85 g (3.5 oz) freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| 1 large can of chopped peeled [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], left to drain over a coarse sieve for 5 minutes\n| 1 tablespoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Garlic powder|garlic powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Mexican oregano]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| Pinch of [[Mixed herbs|mixed herbs]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]] (Guajillo - not too hot)\n| Pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 1 ball of [[Buffalo|buffalo]] [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]], torn\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5), [fan oven 170\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins]\n* Remove the sausagemeat from the sausages and discard the skins\n* Make the [[pizza dough]] as instructed\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Saut\u00e9 the [[onions]], [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and the chorizo sausagemeat in a pan for for about 10 minutes or until the meat is cooked and any liquid has evapourated.  ''There should be enough fat from the sausages not to need any oil.''\n| [[Spray]] or lightly [[Oil|oil]] a deep 25cm (10\") pizza dish or pan\n| Roll out 2/3rds of the [[Dough|dough]] to about 3mm and line a pan so the [[Dough|dough]] just  overlaps the edges and trim any excess\n| Sprinkle the base with the [[Cheddar cheese]]\n| Add the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and [[Chorizo|chorizo]]\n| Sprinkle with one third of the [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| Roll out the remaining [[pizza dough]] to make a lid\n| Pinch the lid so it joins the base and make a few slashed in the top for [[Steam|steam]] to escape\n| Mix another third of the [[Parmesan cheese]] with the [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Spices|spices]] and mix into the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| Spread the tomato mixture over the top of the [[Dough|dough]]\n| Top with crumbled [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] and sprinkle with the remaining [[Parmesan cheese]]\n| [[Bake]] for 45 minutes, resting a sheet of [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]] on top of the [[Pizza|pizza]] for the final 10 minutes\n| Allow to cool for 10 minutes before slicing and serving\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green salad|green salad]]\n===Recipe source===\nInspired by: \n* www.ibelieveicanfry.com/2012/01/chicago-stuffed-pizza.html - now inactive\n* The Chicago Pizza Pie Factory\n* The 1980's!\n===Chef's notes===\nJulia's original used [[Italian]] [[Sausage|sausage]] which I can't get on this snowy winter's day so I've used [[Minced|minced]] [[Chorizo|chorizo]] instead.\n \nIf you don't have garlic powder then just crush a few peeled cloves of garlic and saut\u00e9 them in a little oil for a few minutes, just to take the 'edge' off.\n\nIf you have the time, when sauteeing the onions, etc., you can add back the drained tomato juice little by little and boil it off to create a more intense flavour.  Just ensure the mixture is not too wet before you bake the pizza.\n==See also==\n* www.ibelieveicanfry.com/2012/01/chicago-stuffed-pizza.html Julia's Chicago pizza recipe\n* [[:Category:I believe I can fry recipes|Julia's recipes on Cookipedia]]\n* [http://www.nytimes.com/1994/07/16/obituaries/bob-payton-50-restaurateur-dies.html Bob Payton's obituary (N.Y. Times)]\n* [http://www.independent.co.uk/news/people/obituary-bob-payton-1413990.html Bob Payton's obituary (Independent)]\n* [http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/ShowTopic-g186338-i17-k2760859-Chicago_Pizza_Pie_Factory_in_London-London_England.html Reminiscences from others]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Oh, I so miss this place</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">38 years ago, Chicago Pizza Pie Factory was the place to be.  We used to queue for hours to get in.  This is a pretty close approximation to 'the real thing'!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:I believe I can fry recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#parmesancheese #pizzadough #dried #mushrooms #chicagodeeppanpizza #chorizo #dough #tomatoes #cheddarcheese #grated #mozzarella </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken and Dumplings, Meat recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dumplings #broth #chicken #flour #diced #celery #carrots #chickenanddumplings #onion #dough #rollingpin \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This homemade Chicken and Dumplings recipe, or chicken n\u2019 dumplins\u2019 as it's known in the South, has been added by \u200eDoug Sabulsky, one of our\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 8828\n|PortionCalories = 735\n|DatePublished=13th July 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 12\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  2 hours, 30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  30 minutes\n|CookTime =  2 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken and Dumplings recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice and filling!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">You don't need anything else with this - I couldn't move after a big bowlful of this!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis homemade [[Chicken]] and [[Dumplings]] recipe, or chicken n\u2019 dumplins\u2019 as it's known in the South, has been added by [[User:\u200eDoug Sabulsky|\u200eDoug Sabulsky]], one of our American editors.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n'''[[Broth]] & [[Chicken]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 quarts [[Chicken_stock|Chicken stock]]\n| 4\u00bd pounds [[Chicken thighs]] \n| 5 stalks of [[Celery|celery]], three chopped, two finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 5 [[Carrots]], three chopped, two finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 2 [[Onions]], both peeled.  One quartered, and one finely [[Diced|diced]].\n| 2\u00bd teaspoons [[Black pepper]]\n}}\n'''[[Dumplings]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 cups [[Flour]]\n| \u00be teaspoon [[Baking soda]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt]]\n| 4\u00bd tablespoons Crisco shorting\n| 1\u00bc cups [[Buttermilk]]\n\n}}\n\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n'''[[Broth]] & [[Chicken]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place [[Chicken thighs]] in a large [[Dutch Oven|dutch oven]]. Add [[Chicken]] [[Broth]], the quartered [[Onion]] , three chopped [[Celery]] [[Stocks|stocks]], three chopped [[Carrots]] and 2 teaspoons [[Salt|salt]]. Bring to a [[Boil|boil]]. Reduce heat to a [[Simmer|simmer]], cook covered for one hour.\n| Remove the cooked [[Chicken|chicken]] to cool.  Strain the [[Broth|broth]] and discard the solids, at this point the [[Onion|onion]]/[[Celery|celery]]/[[Carrots|carrots]] have given up all of their flavour in the [[Broth|broth]].  When the [[Chicken|chicken]] is cool, debone and shred the chicken.\n| Add the two finely [[Diced|diced]] [[Carrots|carrots]], two finely [[Diced|diced]] [[Celery|celery]] [[Stocks|stocks]] and the finely diced [[Onion|onion]] back to the [[Strained|strained]] [[Broth|broth]].  Cook [[Broth|broth]] at a low [[Simmer|simmer]] for 30 minutes.\n}}\n'''[[Dumplings]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| While the [[Broth|broth]] is [[Simmering|simmering]], in a bowl, combine the [[Flour|flour]], [[Baking soda|baking soda]], and [[Salt|salt]]. Cut in the [[Shortening|shortening]]. Add the [[Buttermilk|buttermilk]], stirring with a fork until moistened.  [[Knead]] the [[Dough|dough]] 4 to 5 times, and stop.  Do not over work the [[Dough|dough]]!  You are not making [[Bread|bread]].  Over worked dough makes tough [[Dumplings|dumplings]].  The dough should be loose and sticky.\n| You\u0092ll need a [[Rolling pin|rolling pin]] and something to cut the [[Dumplings|dumplings]] with. I like to use a [[Pastry|pastry]] cutter, but a sharp knife works also. I also use a spatula/turner to lift the [[Dumplings|dumplings]] off the cutting surface.\n| On a heavily [[Flour|flour]]ed work surface, roll the [[Dough|dough]] out thin, about &#8539;&#8243; thick with a [[Flour|flour]]ed [[Rolling pin|rolling pin]]. [[Dip]] your cutter in flour and cut the [[Dumplings|dumplings]] in to strips about \u00bd&#8243; x 2&#8243;. It\u0092s okay for them not to be exact. Just eye ball it. Some will be bigger, some smaller, some shaped funny.\n| Use the floured spatula/turner to put them on a heavily floured plate. Just keep flouring between the layers of [[Dumplings|dumplings]]. \n| To cook the [[Dumplings|dumplings]], bring the [[Broth|broth]] to a [[Boil|boil]]. Drop the [[Dumplings|dumplings]] in a few at a time, stirring while you add them. The extra [[Flour|flour]] on them will [[Help|help]] thicken the [[Broth|broth]]. Cook the dumplings for about 15-20 minutes. Stir in the [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and cooked [[Chicken|chicken]], and then serve.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted|Chicken]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dumplings #broth #chicken #flour #diced #celery #carrots #chickenanddumplings #onion #dough #rollingpin </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chicken and Sausage Gumbo",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken and Sausage Gumbo, Meat recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #sausage #okra #chickenandsausagegumbo #roux #flour #gumbo #chickenthighs #onions #stock #vegetables \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Gumbo is a dish that originated in southern Louisiana during the 18th century\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 10907\n|PortionCalories = 908\n|DatePublished=13th July 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 12\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  7 hours, 15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  45 minutes\n|CookTime =  6 hours, 30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken and Sausage Gumbo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Don't like Okra</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">2</span>/5</span>\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Slime in a bowl.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nGumbo is a dish that originated in southern Louisiana during the 18th century. It typically consists primarily of a strongly-flavoured [[stock]], [[meat]] or [[shellfish]], a thickener, and seasoning vegetables, which can include [[celery]], [[bell peppers]] and [[onions]] (a trio known in Cajun cuisine as the \"holy trinity\"). Gumbo is often categorised by the type of thickener used: the African vegetable [[okra]], the Choctaw spice fil\u00e9 powder (dried and ground [[sassafras  leaves]]), or roux, the French base made of flour and fat.\n\nThis version added by [[User:\u200eDoug Sabulsky|\u200eDoug Sabulsky]] is [[Chicken]] and [[Sausage]] [[Gumbo]]\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 cup [[Peanut oil|peanut oil]] \n| 1.5 cups [[Flour|flour]]\n| 2 large [[Onions|onions]], chopped\n| 2 [[Bell peppers|bell peppers]], chopped\n| 4 [[Ribs|ribs]] [[Celery|celery]], chopped\n| 1.5 cups [[Frozen|frozen]] sliced [[Okra|okra]]\n| 4 quarts [[Chicken_stock_(1)|Chicken stock]]\n| 2 [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Creole seasoning]], or to taste\n| 1 teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Thyme leaves|thyme leaves]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n| 1360 g [3 pounds] [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]]\n| 907 g [2 pounds] Andouille [[Sausage|sausage]], cut into 1/2\" pieces\n| 2 cups cut [[Frozen|frozen]] [[Okra|okra]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\nPreheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 175\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 2), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 150\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n''' Method for [[Gumbo]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Season the [[Chicken|chicken]] with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Creole seasoning]], cover and [[Rest for|rest for]] two hours in the [[Refrigerator|refrigerator]].  When ready [[Brown|brown]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] and then [[Brown|brown]] the [[Sausage|sausage]], pour off [[Fat|fat]] and reserve [[Meats|meats]].\n| In a large, heavy pot or cast [[Iron|iron]] [[Skillet|skillet]], heat the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Flour|flour]] over medium heat stirring constantly until thoroughly mixed.   Place the white [[Roux|roux]] into a 350 degree [[Oven|oven]] for one hour or until the [[Roux|roux]] reaches a dark reddish-[[Brown|brown]] colour, or darker ([[Coffee|coffee]] or [[Milk|milk]] [[Chocolate|chocolate]] coloured) for a dark Cajun-style roux.\n| Add the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and stir quickly. This cooks the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and also stops the [[Roux|roux]] from cooking further. Continue to cook, stirring constantly, for about 4 minutes.\n| Add the [[Stock|stock]], seasonings, [[Chicken|chicken]] and [[Sausage|sausage]]. Bring to a [[Boil|boil]], and then cook for about one hour, skimming [[Fat|fat]] off the top as needed.  Remove the [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]], cool, and debone.  Shred the [[Chicken|chicken]] and return to the pot, add the [[Okra|okra]] to heat though, about 15 minutes.\n| Serve with [[White rice|white rice]] and crusty [[French bread]].  Make sure to have plenty of hot [[Sauce|sauce]] and cold [[Beer|beer]] on the table.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes|Chicken]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted|Chicken]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #sausage #okra #chickenandsausagegumbo #roux #flour #gumbo #chickenthighs #onions #stock #vegetables </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]

inch slices.\n| The slices can be [[Toasted|toasted]] on a [[Baking sheet|baking sheet]], or [[Grilled|grilled]] just enough to lightly toast the pieces.\n| Pan [[Fry|fry]] the boneless [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]] in [[Olive oil|olive oil]] with just a little [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| Allow the cooked [[Chicken|chicken]] to cool.\n| [[Dice]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] into large pieces and place into a [[Food processor|food processor]].\n| Add all of the ingredients and [[Blend|blend]] until smooth; it should take about one minute.\n| [[Refrigerate]] for an hour before serving.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nWhen you are ready to serve, add a teaspoon of the [[Pate|pate]] to the [[Baguette|baguette]] slices.\n\nTop with a slice of green [[Olive|olive]].\n\n===Chef's notes===\nI've not seen [[Sausage|sausage]] patties in the UK but the filling from cooked [[Breakfast sausages|breakfast sausages]] or even herby [[Burgers|burgers]] would be a good substitute. --[[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#baguette #chickenandsausagepaterecipe #chickenbreast #chicken #sausage #toasted #refrigerate #foodprocessor #blend #panfried #dice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
